 Udaipur Lok Sabha seat is currently reserved for Scheduled Tribes
 jab yah seat saamaanya hua karti thi tab yahaan sabase zyada teen baar girija vyas saansad raheen
 In the 5 general elections held after independence, this seat was continuously occupied by the Congress
 lekin 1971 main swatantra party ne jeet hasil kii
 So there was a victory of the Bharatiya Lok Dal candidate in the 1977 Janata Lehar
 1980 main congress ke diggaj or purv mukhyamantri mohanlal sukhadiya ne jeet darj kii
 So in the 1984 election, his wife Indubala Sukhadia won
 1989 main bijepi se gulabchand kataaria ne baari maari

 lekin 1998 kaa chunaav girija vyas bijepi ke shantilal chapalot se haar gayi

 lekin 2004 ke loksabhaa chunaav main bijepi kii kiran maheshwari ke saamne girija vyas ko haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa
 In the 2009 elections, this seat became reserved for the Scheduled Castes
 is baar congress ke raghuveer meena saansad bane
 But in the Modi wave of 2014, Raghuveer Meena could not save this seat and became bjp's Arjunlal Meena MP
 saamaajik taana-banajilon kii nagari naam se mashhoor udaipur kaa gauravshaalee itihaas rahaa he

 bihar ke purv mukhyamantri dow
 Jagannath Mishra died in Delhi on Monday at the age of 82
 ve kaaphi lambey samay se beemaari se jujh rahe the
 Dr
 jagannatha mishra bihar kii siyasat main do dashak tak kaddavar cheharaa banakar rahe
 Mishra inherited politics
 unhone apane bade bhai lalit narayan mishra ke nakse par chalate hue congress se apni siyaasi safar kaa aagaaj kiya, lekin vakt ke saath wo badalte gaye or bihar kii siyasat main apni jagah bhi khote gaye
 Dr
 jagannatha mishra kaa janm bihar ke supaul jila ke balua bazaar main 1937 main hua tha
 Jagannath Mishra remained in Congress for a long time
 ve khandaani congressi the
 His elder brother Lalit Narayan Mishra was a veteran Congress leader and a railway minister in the central government
 jagannatha mishra apane bade ke bhai nakshe kadam par chalate hue chaatr jivan main hi bhartiya rashtriya congress se jud gaye the
 Mishra, a strong leader of the Bihar Congress, had learned politics from his elder brother Lalit Narayan Mishra
 jagannatha mishra ne shiksha puri karne ke baad professor ke rup main apana kariyar shuru kiya tha or baad main bihar vishvavidhyalay main arthshaastra ke professor bane
 Even in the academic field, Jagannath Mishra was active in politics
 3 janvari 1975 ko samastipur bam-visphot cond main lalit narayan mishra kii mrityu hone ke baad jagannatha mishra ne apane bade bhai kii siyasat ko aage badhaayaa
 This was the period when Jagannath Mishra got recognition at the national level from the state and came to the center of politics
 ve teen baar bihar ke mukhyamantri bane
 Jagannath Mishra was Chief Minister from 1975 to 1977, 1980 to 1983 and 1989 to 1990
 iske baad 1990 ke dashak ke madhya main kendriya cabinet mantri bhi rahe
 Dr
 in Bihar mishra kaa naam bade netaaon ke taur par janaa jaataa he
 After Mishra, no Congress leader could become the Chief Minister of Bihar
 madhya 90 ke dashak main congress kamjor hone lagi to jagannatha mishra ne sharad pavaar kii party ensipi kaa daaman tham liya
 Although his political stature while in Congress, he could not regain it after his name in the fodder scam
 haalanki jagannatha mishra apane siyaasi varchasv ko dobaaraa se paane ke liye kai raajnneetik daanvpech aajamaae, lekin wo kisi main kaamyaab nahin ho sake
 After NCP, he joined JDU, but could not make his place there too
 2015 ke vidhansabha chunaav ke dauraan balldor se vah bijepi ke netritv vaale endie main entry karnaa chaahate the
 For this, former Chief Minister Jeetan Ram Manjhi laid a political check
 maanjhi ne apane 6 ummidavaaron ke jo naam bijepi ko die the, usamen jagannatha mishra ke bete nitish mishra kaa bhi naam shaamil tha
 After this Jagannath Mishra wrote a book called 'bihar Badar Rahega'
 jiske vimochan main dipti siem susheel modi pahunche the
 In this way, he grew closer to the BJP
 yahi vajah rahi ki jab chaara ghotaale se jagannatha mishra bari hue to argedy ne kaha tha ki bijepi kii kareebi ke vajah se unhen bari kiya gaya he
 Dr
 Jagannath Mishra also met Prime Minister Narendra Modi in 2017
 is dauraan mishra ne pradhanmantri ko 'madhubani-da art capital' pustak kii prati bhent kii thi
 He had asked the Prime Minister to bring to the world an easily accessible information about the civilization, culture, architecture, painting and historical-religious tourist destinations of Mithilanchal region of Bihar

 jaradaari ne kaha ki aatankwaadi is tarah kii ghatnaon ko anjaam dekar logon va sarkaar ke sankalpon ko hilaa nahin sakate
 He said that this incident has given new impetus to the courage of the people to face the threat of terrorism
 raashtrapati ne malala ke jald swasth hone kii kaamana kii or kaha ki puure desh kii shubhakamanaayen uske saath hai
 The Taliban, who were scared of the child, shot dead publicly, saying that Malala is a symbol of the desire of girls of Khyber Pakhtunkhwa province to pursue education
 vah pakistani mahilaon ke barbarta va atyaachaar ke khilaaf khadey hone or use chunauti dene ke saahas kii pratik he

 uske jald swasth hone ke liye sarkaar har sambhav sahaayat karegi

 Rape is a crime of which our society makes our system more guilty than guilty
 kanoon hai, pehle se behatar kanoon hai lekin jo is kanoon ko lagu karte hai ve pulisavaale kya sochate hai balaatkaar jaise sangeen jurm ko lekar

 Legally, the police is looking for rapists but in reality it is finding mistakes in the girl's personal life
 yah kehete hue ki pub kii kamarchaari nahin thi balki graahakon ko vahaan laane kaa kaam karti thi

 zyaadaatar pulisavaalon kaa maananaa he ki balaatkaar ab blakemeling kaa hathiyaar ban chukaa he
 More than 17 officers believe that all this happens for money
 mushkil se ek maheenaa pehle noida police kii joardaar fajihat hui jab usne ek balaatkaar peedit naaballig ladki kii pahchaan ujagar kar di jo chalati car main gangrape kaa shikaar hui thi
 In this case, SP City of Noida had raised questions on the victim girl, but now the extent is reached when the police are saying that if a girl sits in a car with 10 boys, she cannot be innocent? He knows what the consequences of drinking alcohol with boys will be
 balaatkaar ko lekar biimaar soch rakhane vaale pulisavaalon kaa maananaa he ki rape ko lekar sau main se 99 maamle jhuthe hote hai sirf ek se do fisadi cese hi sahi hote hai
 Now consider it a favor to the policemen or you can take this decision better
 
 
 
 No matter how many claims the Delhi Police makes for the safety of women in front of the camera or in front of the public, but if they know what their thinking is off the record, then the people will lose confidence in the police
 sochie! dilli police kaa ek afasar khuleam kah rahaa he ki koi balaatkaar bina ladki ke uksaave ke nahin hota
 There has been debate about what the dress of girls or women should be, from time to time, the contractors of the society have been issuing statements about it
 police ke bade afasar mahilaon ke pahanaave ko lekar tikaa-tippanee karte rahe hai
 Those people may have withdrawn the statement later, but a common policeman who deals with the common people believes that the girls' dress is provoking the men for rape
